\\n21: ## Scheduling and evaluation of alert rules\\n22: \\n23: The scheduling of alert rules happens in the `schedule` package. This package is responsible for managing the evaluation\\n24: of alert rules including checking for new alert rules and stopping the evaluation of deleted alert rules.\\n25: \\n26: The scheduler runs at a fixed interval, called its heartbeat, in which it does a number of tasks:\\n27: \\n28: 1. \\n21: ## Scheduling and evaluation of alert rules\\n22: \\n23: The scheduling of alert rules happens in the `schedule` package. This package is responsible for managing the evaluation\\n24: of alert rules including checking for new alert rules and stopping the evaluation of deleted alert rules.\\n25: \\n26: The scheduler runs at a fixed interval, called its heartbeat, in which it does a number of tasks:\\n27: \\n28: 1. Fetch the alert rules for all organizations (excluding disabled)\\n29: 2. Start a goroutine (if this is a new alert rule or the scheduler has just started) to evaluate the alert rule\\n30: 3. Send an `*evaluation` event to the goroutine for each alert rule if its interval has elapsed\\n31: 4. \n21: ## Scheduling and evaluation of alert rules\n22: \n23: The scheduling of alert rules happens in the `schedule` package. This package is responsible for managing the evaluation\n24: of alert rules including checking for new alert rules and stopping the evaluation of deleted alert rules.\n25: \n26: The scheduler runs at a fixed interval, called its heartbeat, in which it does a number of tasks:\n27: \n28: 1. Fetch the alert rules for all organizations (excluding disabled)\n29: 2. Start a goroutine (if this is a new alert rule or the scheduler has just started) to evaluate the alert rule\n30: 3. Send an `*evaluation` event to the goroutine for each alert rule if its interval has elapsed\n31: 4.
